# Events to rename China/Chinese Imperial empires and to grant temple names to their rulers on death

# by Silverswee(e)per

# TODO: Ming dynasty logic once the history files get to that point
# TODO: Eunuch/GC/etc. law changes on new dynasty

namespace = nameofchina

##### Inheritance

### Inheritance of China within the same dynasty, no longer Chinese Imperial due to wrong religion

# Inform the new EoC, give them the option to convert, and remove all Grace if they don't
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.1
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_1
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_1
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			dynasty = ROOT
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
	
	option = {
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				FROMFROMs_religion_is_playable_trigger = yes
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				FROMFROM = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			religion = FROMFROM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				religion = buddhist
				has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				FROMFROM = {
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			culture = FROMFROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_1 # Convert to Taoist
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				controls_religion = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				trait = zealous
				NOT = {
					true_religion = FROMFROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_1 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				controls_religion = no
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
		}
		
		log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		#log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.2 }
		}
		
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.3 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
}

# Inform the world that all Grace is lost
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.2
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_2
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_2
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_2 # I see...
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}



### Inheritance of China within the same dynasty, suddenly Chinese Imperial

# Inform the new EoC, let them pick a new name for China if China isn't named
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.3
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_3
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_3
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_tang_trigger = yes
			player_or_ai_names_china_tang_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = TANG
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Tang"
			adjective = "Tang"
			set_title_flag = tang_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.4 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_tang_weight = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {

# Inform the world - dynasty name kept
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.6
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_6
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_6
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_6 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}

# Inform the world - new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.7
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_7
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_7
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_7 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}



### Inheritance of China by other dynasty, no longer Chinese Imperial

# Other dynasty inherits - convert?
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.8
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_8
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_8
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
		clr_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		clr_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhou_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = jin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wei_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qi_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = han_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yan_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = zhao_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = liao_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yuan_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = xia_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qing_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = dai_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = cheng_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = liang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = song_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = ming_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = shu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = chu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yue_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = shun_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				FROMFROMs_religion_is_playable_trigger = yes
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				FROMFROM = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			religion = FROMFROM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				religion = buddhist
				has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				FROMFROM = {
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			culture = FROMFROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_8 # Convert
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				controls_religion = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				trait = zealous
				NOT = {
					true_religion = FROMFROM
				}
			}
		}
		
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_8 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				controls_religion = no
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
		}
		
		log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.12 }
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.3 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}

# Inform the world - new dynasty

	id = nameofchina.11
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_11
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_11
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_11 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.14
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_14
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_14
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_14 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

				ai = yes
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_zhao_trigger = yes
			player_or_ai_names_china_zhao_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = ZHAO
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.6 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers if below 3
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Get new Mandate of Heaven level
		
		e_china = {
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Zhao"
			adjective = "Zhao"
			set_title_flag = zhao_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = grace.999 } # Chinese princess (and Grace) update
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.16 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_zhao_weight = yes
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.16 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_chu_weight = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_NAMEOFCHINA_15 # More options!
		clr_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
		set_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
		repeat_event = { id = nameofchina.15 }
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_yue_trigger = yes
			player_or_ai_names_china_yue_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = YUE
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.6 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers if below 3
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Get new Mandate of Heaven level
		
		e_china = {
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Yue"
			adjective = "Yue"
			set_title_flag = yue_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes

		}

# Inform the world - new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.16
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_16
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_16
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_16 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}



### Usurpation/conquest of China by other dynasty, no longer Chinese Imperial due to wrong religion

# Inform the new EoC, give them the option to convert, and reset the name of China if they do not
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.17
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_17
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_17
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
		clr_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		clr_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhou_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = jin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wei_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qi_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = han_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yan_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = zhao_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = liao_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yuan_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = xia_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qing_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = dai_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = cheng_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = liang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = song_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = ming_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = shu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = chu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yue_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = shun_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROM = {
					any_liege = {
						character = ROOT
					]
				}
			]
			FROMFROM = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = king
							tier = duke
						}
						controls_religion = no
					}
					unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				FROMFROMs_religion_is_playable_trigger = yes
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				FROMFROM = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			religion = FROMFROM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				religion = buddhist
				has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				FROMFROM = {
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			culture = FROMFROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_17 # Convert
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				controls_religion = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				trait = zealous
				NOT = {
					true_religion = FROMFROM
				}
			}
		}
		
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.19 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_17 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				controls_religion = no
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
		}
		
		#log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.18 }
		}
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.3 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
}

# Inform the world that all Grace is lost
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.18
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_18
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_18
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_18 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world - new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.20
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_20
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_20
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_20 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

					}

		}

##### Religion conversion

### The EoC converts religion, no longer Chinese Imperial

# Inform the EoC that all Grace will be lost, give the player the option to convert back
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.23
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_23
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_23
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = e_china
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			religion = FROM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				religion = buddhist
				has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			culture = FROM
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_23 # Convert
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				controls_religion = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				trait = zealous
				NOT = {
					true_religion = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_23 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				controls_religion = no
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
		}
		
		log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.24 }
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.3 } # Clean up MoH
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
}

# Inform the world that all Grace is lost if the EoC picks that option
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.24
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_24
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_24
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_24 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}



### The EoC converts religion/culture, now Chinese Imperial, China not named

# Inform the EoC, let them pick a new name for China
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.25
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_25
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_25

		}
		has_landed_title = e_china

				has_title_flag = wu_china

				has_title_flag = yin_china
				has_title_flag = shun_china
			}
		}
	}

	}
	
	# Please select new China name!

		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Get new Mandate of Heaven level

			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
		}

			set_name = "Tang"
			adjective = "Tang"

		}
		
		if = {

					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty

					}
				}
				NOT = {

				}
			}

		}

			factor = 1
			name_china_tang_weight = yes
		}
	}

				ai = yes

narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.26
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_26
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_26
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_26 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}



### The EoC converts religion, now Chinese Imperial, China named

# Inform the EoC
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.27
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_27
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_27
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = taoist_convert
			}
		}
		has_landed_title = e_china
		# China is already named
		e_china = {
			OR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china
				has_title_flag = jin_china
				has_title_flag = wei_china
				has_title_flag = qi_china
				has_title_flag = zhou_china
				has_title_flag = han_china
				has_title_flag = qin_china
				has_title_flag = yan_china
				has_title_flag = zhao_china
				has_title_flag = liao_china
				has_title_flag = yuan_china
				has_title_flag = xia_china
				has_title_flag = qing_china
				has_title_flag = dai_china
				has_title_flag = cheng_china
				has_title_flag = liang_china
				has_title_flag = song_china
				has_title_flag = ming_china
				has_title_flag = shu_china
				has_title_flag = wu_china
				has_title_flag = chu_china
				has_title_flag = yue_china
				has_title_flag = yin_china
				has_title_flag = shun_china
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_27 # Inform the world
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.28 }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.28
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_28
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_28
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_28 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}

##### Extra

### Name reset

# Non-Taoist gets e_china from non-dynastic non-Taoist
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.29
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
			OR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china
				has_title_flag = jin_china
				has_title_flag = wei_china
				has_title_flag = qi_china
				has_title_flag = zhou_china
				has_title_flag = han_china
				has_title_flag = qin_china
				has_title_flag = yan_china
				has_title_flag = zhao_china
				has_title_flag = liao_china
				has_title_flag = yuan_china
				has_title_flag = xia_china
				has_title_flag = qing_china
				has_title_flag = dai_china
				has_title_flag = cheng_china
				has_title_flag = liang_china
				has_title_flag = song_china
				has_title_flag = ming_china
				has_title_flag = shu_china
				has_title_flag = wu_china
				has_title_flag = chu_china
				has_title_flag = yue_china
				has_title_flag = yin_china
				has_title_flag = shun_china
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		e_china = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}


##### Pretender empires

### Creation

# The holder gets to pick a name
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.30
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_30
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_30
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
	}
	
	# Please select new China name!
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_tang_trigger = yes
			player_or_ai_names_china_tang_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = TANG
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.6 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers if below 3
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Get new Mandate of Heaven level
		
		primary_title = {
			set_short_name = no
			set_name = "Tang"
			adjective = "Tang"
			set_title_flag = tang_china
			add_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_FAKE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = special_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = special_chinese_imperial
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.31 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_tang_weight = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}

			}
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = special_chinese_imperial
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.31 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_chu_weight = yes
		}
	}

			has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6

# Inform the world
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.31
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_31
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_31
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = no
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_31 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_31 # Down with the upstarts!
	}
}

### Destroy any empire if the EoC inherits it (or any non-e_china title if its holder becomes the EoC)

# Destroy the title
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.32
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_32
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_32
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			tier = emperor
			is_china_or_pretender_empire_trigger = yes
		}
		government = chinese_imperial_government
		NOR = {
			has_character_flag = recreated_china
			has_character_flag = forming_india
			has_character_flag = restoring_rome
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = special_usurpation
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_32 # The Middle Kingdom is enough!
		
		# Keep China if you have it
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = e_china
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					NOT = {
						title = e_china
					}
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_nicaea
							title = e_lechczechrus
							title = e_golden_horde
							title = e_il-khanate
							title = e_mongol_empire
							title = e_timurids
							title = e_hre
							title = e_roman_empire
							title = e_byzantium
							title = e_wendish_empire
							title = e_russia
							title = e_pontic_steppe
							title = e_persia
							title = e_arabia
							title = e_maghreb
							title = e_seljuk_turks
							title = e_latin_empire
							title = e_mexikha
							title = e_bengal
							title = e_deccan
							title = e_khmer
							title = e_pacific_rim
							title = e_great_wall
							title = e_black_turtle
							title = e_white_tiger
							title = e_yellow_dragon
							title = e_azure_dragon
							title = e_vermilion_bird
							title = e_jade_gate
							title = e_northern_steppe
							title = e_golden_river
							title = e_treasure_fleet
							title = e_tawantinsuyu
							title = e_northern_plain
							title = e_eastern_reaches
						}
					}
					set_short_name = yes
				}
				clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
		}
		# Or keep a title matching your bloodline
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = emperor
					title_matches_my_chinese_bloodline_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			# First destroy unmatching titles
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					title_matches_my_chinese_bloodline_trigger = no
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_nicaea
							title = e_lechczechrus
							title = e_golden_horde
							title = e_il-khanate
							title = e_mongol_empire
							title = e_timurids
							title = e_hre
							title = e_roman_empire
							title = e_byzantium
							title = e_wendish_empire
							title = e_russia
							title = e_pontic_steppe
							title = e_persia
							title = e_arabia
							title = e_maghreb
							title = e_seljuk_turks
							title = e_latin_empire
							title = e_mexikha
							title = e_bengal
							title = e_deccan
							title = e_khmer
							title = e_pacific_rim
							title = e_great_wall
							title = e_black_turtle
							title = e_white_tiger
							title = e_yellow_dragon
							title = e_azure_dragon
							title = e_vermilion_bird
							title = e_jade_gate
							title = e_northern_steppe
							title = e_golden_river
							title = e_treasure_fleet
							title = e_tawantinsuyu
							title = e_northern_plain
							title = e_eastern_reaches
						}
					}
					set_short_name = yes
				}
				clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
			# Then destroy non-primary empires, if we somehow ended up with two pretender empires
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							NOT = {
								title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_nicaea
							title = e_lechczechrus
							title = e_golden_horde
							title = e_il-khanate
							title = e_mongol_empire
							title = e_timurids
							title = e_hre
							title = e_roman_empire
							title = e_byzantium
							title = e_wendish_empire
							title = e_russia
							title = e_pontic_steppe
							title = e_persia
							title = e_arabia
							title = e_maghreb
							title = e_seljuk_turks
							title = e_latin_empire
							title = e_mexikha
							title = e_bengal
							title = e_deccan
							title = e_khmer
							title = e_pacific_rim
							title = e_great_wall
							title = e_black_turtle
							title = e_white_tiger
							title = e_yellow_dragon
							title = e_azure_dragon
							title = e_vermilion_bird
							title = e_jade_gate
							title = e_northern_steppe
							title = e_golden_river
							title = e_treasure_fleet
							title = e_tawantinsuyu
							title = e_northern_plain
							title = e_eastern_reaches
						}
					}
					set_short_name = yes
				}
				clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
		}
		# Or just keep your primary title
		else = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							NOT = {
								title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_nicaea
							title = e_lechczechrus
							title = e_golden_horde
							title = e_il-khanate
							title = e_mongol_empire
							title = e_timurids
							title = e_hre
							title = e_roman_empire
							title = e_byzantium
							title = e_wendish_empire
							title = e_russia
							title = e_pontic_steppe
							title = e_persia
							title = e_arabia
							title = e_maghreb
							title = e_seljuk_turks
							title = e_latin_empire
							title = e_mexikha
							title = e_bengal
							title = e_deccan
							title = e_khmer
							title = e_pacific_rim
							title = e_great_wall
							title = e_black_turtle
							title = e_white_tiger
							title = e_yellow_dragon
							title = e_azure_dragon
							title = e_vermilion_bird
							title = e_jade_gate
							title = e_northern_steppe
							title = e_golden_river
							title = e_treasure_fleet
							title = e_tawantinsuyu
							title = e_northern_plain
							title = e_eastern_reaches
						}
					}
					set_short_name = yes
				}
				clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
		}
	}

### Pretender empire changes hands

# Stop being pretender empire (AI picks this if NOT of FROMFROM's dynasty)?
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.33
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_33
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_33
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = special_usurpation
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_33 # Keep being a pretender empire!
		
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		
		FROM = {
			make_primary_title = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
				NOT = {
					title = FROM
				}
			}
			unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = nameofchina.35 } # Rename the empire
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
				e_china = {
					has_holder = yes
					holder_scope = {
						is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						OR = {
							has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
							has_bloodline_flag = pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_33 # Stop being a pretender empire!
		
		FROM = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							title = e_nicaea
							title = e_lechczechrus
							title = e_golden_horde
							title = e_il-khanate
							title = e_mongol_empire
							title = e_timurids
							title = e_hre
							title = e_roman_empire
							title = e_byzantium
							title = e_wendish_empire
							title = e_russia
							title = e_pontic_steppe
							title = e_persia
							title = e_arabia
							title = e_maghreb
							title = e_seljuk_turks
							title = e_latin_empire
							title = e_mexikha
							title = e_bengal
							title = e_deccan
							title = e_khmer
							title = e_pacific_rim
							title = e_great_wall
							title = e_black_turtle
							title = e_white_tiger
							title = e_yellow_dragon
							title = e_azure_dragon
							title = e_vermilion_bird
							title = e_jade_gate
							title = e_northern_steppe
							title = e_golden_river
							title = e_treasure_fleet
							title = e_tawantinsuyu
							title = e_northern_plain
							title = e_eastern_reaches
						}
					}
					set_short_name = yes
				}
			remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
			clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}

		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.34 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				dynasty = FROMFROM
				controls_religion = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					e_china = {
						OR = {
							has_holder = no
							holder_scope = {
								is_chinese_emperor_trigger = no
							}
						}
					}
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						OR = {
							has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
							has_bloodline_flag = pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline
						}
					}
				}
				can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.3 } # Clean up MoH modifiers
	}
}

# Inform the world if the pretender empire stops being a pretender empire
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.34
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_34
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_34
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = no
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_34 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_34 # As it should be!
	}
}

				text = CREATE_FAKE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_min_weight = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_35 # Keep using the existing dynasty name!
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Get new Mandate of Heaven level
		
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_NAMEOFCHINA_35 # More options! (Restart)
		clr_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
		repeat_event = { id = nameofchina.35 }
	}
}

# on_death event to set temple names
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.36
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		real_tier = emperor # This ensures vassal kinsmen of the EoC aren't included
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Historical EoCs (that held e_china) get their historical temple name
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_daizong
			}
			set_name = "Daizong"
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_dezong
			}

			set_character_flag = temple_name_given

##### Various pings to fix scopes

# Inheritance within same dynasty - suddenly Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.37
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			dynasty = ROOT
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		# China isn't already named
		e_china = {
			NOR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china
				has_title_flag = jin_china
				has_title_flag = wei_china
				has_title_flag = qi_china
				has_title_flag = zhou_china
				has_title_flag = han_china
				has_title_flag = qin_china
				has_title_flag = yan_china
				has_title_flag = zhao_china
				has_title_flag = liao_china
				has_title_flag = yuan_china
				has_title_flag = xia_china
				has_title_flag = qing_china
				has_title_flag = dai_china
				has_title_flag = cheng_china
				has_title_flag = liang_china
				has_title_flag = song_china
				has_title_flag = ming_china
				has_title_flag = shu_china
				has_title_flag = wu_china
				has_title_flag = chu_china
				has_title_flag = yue_china
				has_title_flag = yin_china
				has_title_flag = shun_china
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.3 days = 1 } # Fire the actual event
	}
}

# Inheritance by other dynasty
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.38
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.5 days = 1 } # Fire the actual event
	}
}

# Usurpation/conquest by other dynasty
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.39
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = special_usurpation
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.13 days = 1 } # Fire the actual event
	}
}

		}

		}
		# China isn't already named
		e_china = {
			NOR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china
				has_title_flag = jin_china
				has_title_flag = wei_china
				has_title_flag = qi_china
				has_title_flag = zhou_china
				has_title_flag = han_china
				has_title_flag = qin_china
				has_title_flag = yan_china
				has_title_flag = zhao_china
				has_title_flag = liao_china
				has_title_flag = yuan_china
				has_title_flag = xia_china
				has_title_flag = qing_china

				has_title_flag = cheng_china
				has_title_flag = liang_china
				has_title_flag = song_china
				has_title_flag = ming_china
				has_title_flag = shu_china
				has_title_flag = wu_china
				has_title_flag = chu_china
				has_title_flag = yue_china
				has_title_flag = yin_china
				has_title_flag = shun_china
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.21 days = 1 } # Fire the actual event
	}
}

# on_startup event to set the relevant flag(s)
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.42
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
	} 
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = e_china
			}
			update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
			}
			add_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# on_death event ensuring that dead Song emperors have their zhangokfutou
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.43
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		government = chinese_imperial_government
		OR = {
			dynasty = 1051151 ### Song Dynasty, known in almost all official artwork as wearing their weird zhangokfutou
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = song_china # If someone creates a "Song", give them the proper headgear!
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_trait = dead_song_emperor
	}
}

# A Chinese Imperial China was created - inform the world
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.44
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_44
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_44
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_44 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}


# Inform the new EoC, let them pick a new name for China
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.45
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_45
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_45
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_tang_trigger = yes
			player_or_ai_names_china_tang_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = TANG
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.6 } # Clean up Mandate of Heaven modifiers if below 3
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Get new Mandate of Heaven level
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Tang"
			adjective = "Tang"
			set_title_flag = tang_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.44 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			name_china_tang_weight = yes
		}
	}

# Cleanup prior to nameofchina.45
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.46
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# Clear out Grace, Grace-related modifiers, and Chinese Princesses (even if ROOT happens to share the dynasty of the last EoC)
		hidden_tooltip = {
			# Clear out Chinese princesses that somehow had that trait
			any_character = { # Performance-intensitve, but necessary here
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						dynasty = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
				remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
			}
			# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
			any_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = grace_character
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = grace
					value = 0
				}
				clr_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			
			#log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
			
			# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
			any_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
				}
				remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			
			#log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
			
			## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
			#any_character = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
			#	}
			#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
			#}
			#
			##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
			
			# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
			any_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
				}
				remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			
			#log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
			
			# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
			any_character = {
				limit = {
					has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
				}
				remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
		}
		
		# Assign traits to new Chinese princesses
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					name = imperial_marriages
					value = enabled
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						is_married = no
						is_consort = no
						NOR = {
							trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
							trait = dragon_bride_married # If married off but no longer married, don't add the trait again!
						}
						host = {
							OR = {
								character = ROOT
								any_liege = {
									OR = {
										character = ROOT
										liege_before_war = {
											character = ROOT
										}
									}
								}
								liege_before_war = {
									character = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						is_female = yes
						is_married = yes
					}
					add_trait = dragon_bride_married
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Clear the name of China
		e_china = {
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			grant_title = ROOT
			make_primary_title = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
			}
			character_event = { id = nameofchina.45 } # Pick a new name for China
		}
	}
}

# Tributaries of China are transferred but have their tier lowered on usurpation
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.47
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Since China no longer can revoke titles for no reason, make sure the capital is transferred properly
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					capital_scope = {
						holder_scope = {
							top_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
							NOT = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				capital_scope = {
					county = {
						usurp_title = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# Decrease tributary tier or free them entirely
		FROMFROM = {
			any_tributary = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_tributary = {
								type = chinese_client_state
							}
							is_tributary = {
								type = chinese_protectorate
							}
							is_tributary = {
								type = chinese_imperial_tributary
							}
							is_tributary = {
								type = chinese_peripheral_tributary
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PREV = {
								dynasty = ROOT
							}
						}
						decrease_tributary_tier_or_release_effect = yes
						# TODO: Actual event alerting the tributary
						# TODO: Actual event alerting the former suzerain
						# TODO: Actual event alerting ROOT
					}
					else = {
						PREV = {
							remove_tributary = PREV
							# TODO: Actual event alerting the tributary
							# TODO: Actual event alerting the former suzerain
							# TODO: Actual event alerting ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROM = {
					any_liege = {
						character = ROOT
					]
				}
			]
			FROMFROM = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = king
							tier = duke
						}
						controls_religion = no
					}
					unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### A pretender converts, no longer Chinese Imperial

# Inform the pretender that Chinese Imperial is lost, give the player the option to convert back
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.48
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_48
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_48
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
	
	trigger = {
		primary_title = {
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		ROOT = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			religion = FROM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				religion = buddhist
				has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
				FROM = {
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			culture = FROM
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_48 # Convert
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				controls_religion = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = no
				trait = zealous
				NOT = {
					true_religion = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_48 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_only_religion_trigger = yes
					has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				controls_religion = no
				NOT = {
					trait = zealous
				}
			}
		}
		
		primary_title = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						title = e_nicaea
						title = e_lechczechrus
						title = e_golden_horde
						title = e_il-khanate
						title = e_mongol_empire
						title = e_timurids
						title = e_hre
						title = e_roman_empire
						title = e_byzantium
						title = e_wendish_empire
						title = e_russia
						title = e_pontic_steppe
						title = e_persia
						title = e_arabia
						title = e_maghreb
						title = e_seljuk_turks
						title = e_latin_empire
						title = e_mexikha
						title = e_bengal
						title = e_deccan
						title = e_khmer
						title = e_pacific_rim
						title = e_great_wall
						title = e_black_turtle
						title = e_white_tiger
						title = e_yellow_dragon
						title = e_azure_dragon
						title = e_vermilion_bird
						title = e_jade_gate
						title = e_northern_steppe
						title = e_golden_river
						title = e_treasure_fleet
						title = e_tawantinsuyu
						title = e_northern_plain
						title = e_eastern_reaches
					}
				}
				set_short_name = yes
			}
			remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
			clear_all_chinese_name_title_flags_effect = yes
			clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}

		make_me_feudal_effect = yes
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.34 }
		}
		character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.3 } # Clean up MoH modifiers
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
}

##### Force Chinese Imperial at the start for all relevant rulers

character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.50
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			primary_title = { has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire }
			has_landed_title = e_china
			any_liege = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
					}
					liege_before_war = {
						dynasty = ROOT
						is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			liege_before_war = {
				dynasty = ROOT
				is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		is_patrician = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		#set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		log = "[Root.GetBestName] is now properly Chinese Imperial!"
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				real_tier = emperor
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_1
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					duration = -1
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_1
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Lost!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_2
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					duration = -1
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_2
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Poor!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_3
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					duration = -1
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_3
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Average!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_4
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					duration = -1
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_4
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Good!"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = moh_5
				}
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					duration = -1
				}
				set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
				clr_character_flag = moh_5
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Unquestioned!"
			}
			else = {
				set_character_flag = fallback_starting_mandate_set
				log = "[Root.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating will use the fallback option!"
				character_event = { id = mandate_of_heaven.1 } # Add a relevant MoH modifier
			}
			character_event = { id = soh.5301 } # Generate starting Court Eunuchs
		}
	}
}
